\hypertarget{structed__state__vars_1_1edtype}{}\doxysection{ed\+\_\+state\+\_\+vars\+::edtype Type Reference}
\label{structed__state__vars_1_1edtype}\index{ed\_state\_vars::edtype@{ed\_state\_vars::edtype}}


Contains arrays of polygons that populate the current grid. This is the most averaged and least nested dimension.

\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
Contains arrays of polygons that populate the current grid. This is the most averaged and least nested dimension.
